[11/10/18, 11:43:29â€¯AM] â€ª+91Â 95919Â 89838â€¬: Need advice please on a land sale transaction:

Buyer is buying one half of a one acre land parcel. Can a sale deed be registered PRIOR TO bifurcation of the land by simply mentioning in the sale deed that one half of the land is being sold (the owner will attach a site plan showing the area which is to be sold)? The owner maintains that the buyer, POST registration of the sale deed, can take the khata certificate from BBMP for his portion of the land.

[11/10/18, 11:48:20â€¯AM] â€ª+91Â 91Â 0Â 80766Â 66â€¬: Good morning 
You need to make a amendment of plan in car and to the actual scale from cad centre or architect and mention that as part of sale deed terms clearly that it's a split sale and register that document at sub registrar document and show it.

Example of SY no 10 being original and it's been split like Sy no 10/1 & 10/2 as 2 part sale.

You must have a advocate to do this job. Which I feel you have not engaged now. Word of caution; Never do documentation and drafting by yourself and through drafting agents but use a competitive advocate and pay a price for it. Its worth it. 

Regards 

Madhu Sudan
